# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
we define the unit cost as the cost of producing a certain quantity of product, while the
marginal cost as the increase or decrease in the unit cost with the change of quantity of product ^NmAEYKCi

if f is concave up, the first derivative has a positive gradient, so the second derivative is
positive because the gradient of f is always growing.
if f is concave down, the first derivative has negative gradient so the second derivative is
negative because the gradient of f is always decreasing ^l3in6fho

on a local max the first derivative goes from positive to negative but the second remain
negative.
on a local min, the first derivative goes from negative to positive but the second remain
positive.
on a points of inflection the concavity change, the first derivative touches 0 but remain
of the same sign, while the second goes from positive to negative when going from concave up
to concave down or vice versa ^oPuWAifG

also, at a local maximum the curve is concave down, so the gradient of the first derivative
is decreasing, so if the second derivative at a stationary point is negative the point is a local
max, reversed for a local min ^HSThhiRH
